\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_ecall_ConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf void} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_ab1863bdc62d46e8cf945b3e2fa92f556}{}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_ab1863bdc62d46e8cf945b3e2fa92f556}
Connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Block until the service is available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Create}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}

\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}

Create a new e\+Call object

The e\+Call is not actually established at this point. It\textquotesingle{}s still up to the caller to call le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Start() when ready.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item A reference to the new Call object.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On failure, the process exits; you don\textquotesingle{}t have to worry about checking the returned reference for validity. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Disconnect the current client thread from the service providing this A\+PI.

Normally, this function doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to be called. After this function is called, there\textquotesingle{}s no longer a connection to the service, and the functions in this A\+PI can\textquotesingle{}t be used. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically. \index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+End@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+End}}

\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode(void)}{le_ecall_ExitOnlyMode(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Exit\+Only\+Mode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_a924114fa7fab10c3f351766a76134f34}{}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_a924114fa7fab10c3f351766a76134f34}
This function exits from e\+Call Only mode. It configures the e\+Call operation mode to Normal mode, the modem uses the default operation mode at power up (or after U/\+S\+IM hotswap). The modem behaves following the U/\+S\+IM e\+Call operation mode; for example the U/\+S\+IM can be configured only for e\+Call, or a combination of e\+Call and commercial service provision.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode(void)}{le_ecall_ForceOnlyMode(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Force\+Only\+Mode (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_a042d52c84b5b679ab32dd814c5b0be9e}{}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_a042d52c84b5b679ab32dd814c5b0be9e}
This function configures the e\+Call operation mode to e\+Call only, only emergency number can be used to start an e\+Call session. The modem doesn\textquotesingle{}t try to register on the Cellular network. This function forces the modem to behave as e\+Call only mode whatever U/\+S\+IM operation mode. The change doesn\textquotesingle{}t persist over power cycles. This function can be called before making an e\+Call.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT for other failures
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+S\+U\+P\+P\+O\+R\+T\+ED Not supported on this platform 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

Import an already prepared M\+SD.

M\+SD is transmitted only after an emergency call has been established.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+O\+V\+E\+R\+F\+L\+OW The imported M\+SD length exceeds the M\+S\+D\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+L\+EN maximum length.

\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT for other failures
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
On failure, the process exits; you don\textquotesingle{}t have to worry about checking the returned reference for validity. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Set the E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+E\+M\+P\+TS value. If a dial attempt under automatic emergency call initiation failed, it should be repeated maximally E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+A\+U\+T\+O\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+A\+T\+T\+E\+M\+P\+T\+S-\/1 times within the maximal time limit of E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+U\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON. The default value is 10. Redial attempts stop once the call has been cleared down correctly, or if counter/timer reached their limits.

\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on failure 
\end{DoxyItemize}

Set the E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+D\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+D\+U\+R\+A\+T\+I\+ON time. It\textquotesingle{}s the maximum time the I\+VS have to connect the emergency call to the P\+S\+AP, including all redial attempts. If the call is not connected within this time (or Manual\+Dial\+Attempts/\+Auto\+Dial\+Attempts dial attempts), it will stop.

Set the E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+C\+C\+FT time. It\textquotesingle{}s the maximum delay before initiating an an automatic call termination. When the delay is reached and I\+VS N\+AD didn\textquotesingle{}t receive a call clear-\/down indication then the call is immediatly terminated.

Allowed range of values is 1 to 720 minutes.
\end{DoxyNote}

Set the position transmitted by the M\+SD.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+U\+P\+L\+I\+C\+A\+TE an M\+SD has been already imported
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+B\+A\+D\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+M\+E\+T\+ER bad input parameter
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT on other failures
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
The process exits, if an invalid e\+Call reference is given 
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em ecall\+Ref} & e\+Call reference \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em is\+Trusted} & true if the position is accurate, false otherwise \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em latitude} & latitude in degrees with 6 decimal places, positive North. Maximum value is +90 degrees (+90000000), minimum value is -\/90 degrees (-\/90000000). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em longitude} & longitude in degrees with 6 decimal places, positive East. Maximum value is +180 degrees (+180000000), minimum value is -\/180 degrees (-\/180000000). \\
\hline
\mbox{\tt in}  & {\em direction} & direction of the vehicle from magnetic north (0 to 358, clockwise) in 2-\/degrees unit. Valid range is 0 to 179. If direction of travel is invalid or unknown, the value 0x\+FF shall be used. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service(void)}{le_ecall_TryConnectService(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Try\+Connect\+Service (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_ab546b43bee315c4cfc2d5697cad3cf4b}{}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_ab546b43bee315c4cfc2d5697cad3cf4b}
Try to connect the current client thread to the service providing this A\+PI. Return with an error if the service is not available.

For each thread that wants to use this A\+PI, either Connect\+Service or Try\+Connect\+Service must be called before any other functions in this A\+PI. Normally, Connect\+Service is automatically called for the main thread, but not for any other thread. For details, see \hyperlink{apiFilesC_apiFilesC_client}{Client-\/specific Functions}.

This function is created automatically.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK if the client connected successfully to the service.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+U\+N\+A\+V\+A\+I\+L\+A\+B\+LE if the server is not currently offering the service to which the client is bound.
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+N\+O\+T\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+M\+I\+T\+T\+ED if the client interface is not bound to any service (doesn\textquotesingle{}t have a binding).
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+M\+M\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+OR if the Service Directory cannot be reached. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers}}
\index{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers}!le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h@{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+interface.\+h}}
\subsubsection[{\texorpdfstring{le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers(void)}{le_ecall_UseUSimNumbers(void)}}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}{\bf le\+\_\+result\+\_\+t} le\+\_\+ecall\+\_\+\+Use\+U\+Sim\+Numbers (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{{\bf void}}]{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}\hypertarget{le__ecall__interface_8h_a034c442fd7c6650ed956822a561c0104}{}\label{le__ecall__interface_8h_a034c442fd7c6650ed956822a561c0104}
When modem is in E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+F\+O\+R\+C\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+S\+I\+S\+T\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE or E\+C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+O\+N\+L\+Y\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE, this function can be called to request the modem to read the number to dial from the F\+D\+N/\+S\+DN of the U/\+S\+IM.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
If F\+DN directory is updated with new dial numbers, be sure that the S\+IM card is refreshed.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+OK on success
\item L\+E\+\_\+\+F\+A\+U\+LT for other failures 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
